 haalanki yahaan sawaal yah uthta he ki agar kisi ke saath aisa haadasa hota he, to kya amusment park or uske management ke khilaaf cese kiya ja saktaa he?supreme court baar association ke upaadhyaksh jitendra mohan sharma or edwocket kalika prasad kaala ‘maanas’ kaa kahana he ki agar amusment park main kisi bhi tarah kaa haadasa hota he yaa jhula tuutata he or usamen amusment park management kii laaparvaahee (negligence) pai jaati he, to civil cese kiya ja saktaa he
 In such a case, tortious liability is created on the amusement park
 is tarah ke maamle main nyaayalay amusment park management kii laaparvaahee or peedit ko hue nuksaan kaa aankalan karata he or iske baad muaavja kii raashi tay karata he
 Advocate Kala says that the amusement park cannot be held responsible if the accident happens due to the fault or negligence of the victim
 iskaa matlab yah he ki agar jhula se jaanboojhkar koi kud jaataa he, to aise maamle main amusment park management kii laaparvaahee nahin hoti he or na hi torts libility banati he
 Therefore, the victim cannot be compensated in any way
 kab amusment park management hoga laaparvaahee kaa doshijab sawaal kiya gaya ki is baat kaa pataa kaise chalegaa ki kisi haadase kii vajah amusment park management kii laaparvaahee he yaa nahin? is par supreme court ke senior edwocket jitendra mohan sharma or edwocket kalika prasad kaala ‘maanas’ ne kaha ki amusment park management kii legal duty he ki wo vahaan aane waalon ko surakshit maahaul uplabdh karaae, unki puri care kare or puri satarkta barte
 If he does not do so, he will be held guilty of negligence
 inke mutabik amusment park kii laaparvaahee kaa pataa in aadhaaron par lagaaya ja saktaa he
 
 
 1
 amusment park management ne vahaan aane vaale logon kii suraksha ke liye sabhi jaruri kadam uthaae hai yaa nahin? agar amusment park management suraksha ke sabhi jaruri kadam nahin uthaata he, to usko laaparvaahee kaa doshi tehraaya ja saktaa he
 2
 amusment park or vahaan kii mashiinon kii samay par marammat kii gai he yaa nahin? agar amusment park or vahaan istemaal hone vaali mashiinon kii samay par marammat nahin kii gai, to amusment park ko laaparvaahee kaa jimmedaar tehraaya ja saktaa he
 3
 amusment park management ko vahaan aane vaale logon ko suraksha upaay (safety measure) se avgat karana hoga
 If the amusement park management does not do so and any injury or death occurs to the visitor, then the amusement park management will be held liable for negligence
 4
 All rules and laws must be followed in the operation of an amusement park
 agar park management kisi bhi tarah ke niyamon yaa kanoonon kaa ulanghan karata he, to iske liye usko laaparvaahee kaa doshi tehraaya ja saktaa he
 Amusement Park will not be responsible for your mistake
 Senior Advocate Jitendra Mohan Sharma and Advocate Kalika Prasad Kala 'manas' say that if an Amusement Park does not follow the safety rules as instructed by the management and any accident occurs due to it For such an accident, the person himself will be responsible
 duusare kii galati ke liye park management ko jimmedaar nahin tehraaya ja saktaa he
 This is a good defense for park management
 bharat main lau of tortedwocket kalika prasad kaa kahana he ki lau of tort kaaphi advance sosayadi kaa kanoon he
 It is rarely used in India
 haalanki negligence ke maamalon main iskaa istemaal khub dekhne ko miltaa he
 Apart from this, Jitendra Mohan Sharma, Senior Advocate of the Supreme Court, says that till now the Law of Tort has not developed as much as it should
 haalanki ab yah dhire-dhire develop hone laga he or jaldi hi bharat main iskaa khub istemaal hone lagegaa
 Criminal Case against Amusement Park, Senior Advocate of the Supreme Court Jitendra Mohan Sharma says that if Amusement Park is negligent and does not perform its legal duty and someone gets hurt or dies, then against Amusement Park Management Criminal cases can also be brought
 agar isamen kisi kii maut hoti he to bhartiya dand samhita yani ipisi kii dhara 304 e ke tahat maamla darj karaayaa ja saktaa he
 Under this, a provision of 2 years jail and fine has been made
 iske alaava laaparvaahee baratane par amusment park management ke khilaaf ipisi kii dhara 336, 337 or 338 ke tahat maamla darj karaayaa ja saktaa he
 These sections have the provision of imprisonment ranging from 3 months to 2 years and fine

 The South African batsmen set several records in the pool match of the ICC World Cup 2015 held at Manuka Oval ground with Ireland on Tuesday
 salaami ballebaaj hashim amala ne 159 ranon kii shandaar pari kheli
 This is the 20th century of his career
 amala ne sabase kam maichon main 20waan shatak lagane kebharat ke viraat kohli ke record kodhwast kiya
 Amla completed his 20th century in the 108th innings of his 111th career
 kohli ne apane kariyarke 141wein match kii 133veen pari main yah mukaam hasil kiya tha
 In this way Amla shattered Kohli's record by a margin of 25 innings
 amala ekadivasiy maichon main 20 yaa usase adhik shatak lagane vaale vishwa ke 12wein ballebaaj ban gaye
 After Herschelle Gibbs, Amla is the second player jointly with current captain Abraham de Villiers to score the most centuries for South Africa

 The record of the most centuries in odis is in the name of India's Sachin Tendulkar
 sachin ne 49 shatak lagaae hai
 Amla and Faf du Plessis (109) shared a record partnership of 247 runs for the second wicket against Ireland
 yah vishwa cap itihaas main south africa ke liye kisi bhi wicket ke liye duusari sabase badi saajhedaari he

 is wicket ke liye south africa kii ore se teesri sabase badi saajhedaari bhi amala or plasis ke hi naam he

 saath hi yah vishwa cap itihaas kii ab tak kii paanchavin sabase badi saajhedaari he

 - Now uninstall whatsapp from your device
